              <section class="elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-7edbe77 elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-element_type="section" data-id="7edbe77">
               <div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
                <div class="elementor-row">
                 <div class="elementor-column elementor-col-100 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-1bc0387" data-element_type="column" data-id="1bc0387">
                  <div class="elementor-column-wrap elementor-element-populated">
                   <div class="elementor-widget-wrap">
                    <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-2874329 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="2874329" data-widget_type="heading.default">
                     <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                      <h1 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">
                       Rulings
                      </h1>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-3995e21 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="3995e21" data-widget_type="heading.default">
                     <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                      <h1 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">
                       by LORRAINE BAILEY
                      </h1>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <section class="elementor-section elementor-inner-section elementor-element elementor-element-5ccb0ae elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-element_type="section" data-id="5ccb0ae" id="rulings">
                     <div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
                      <div class="elementor-row">
                       <div class="elementor-column elementor-col-20 elementor-inner-column elementor-element elementor-element-3585f8f" data-element_type="column" data-id="3585f8f">
                        <div class="elementor-column-wrap elementor-element-populated">
                         <div class="elementor-widget-wrap">
                          <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-0454cf6 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="0454cf6" data-widget_type="heading.default">
                           <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                            <h1 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">
                             <a data-wpel-link="internal" href="https://www.courthousenews.com/organic-food-labeling/" rel="follow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                              Organic Food Labeling
                             </a>
                            </h1>
                           </div>
                          </div>
                          <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-cc9ffa5 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-element_type="widget" data-id="cc9ffa5" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
                           <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                            <div class="elementor-text-editor elementor-clearfix">
                             <p>
                              A federal judge
                              <strong>
                               <a data-wpel-link="internal" href="https://www.courthousenews.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/organic-labeling.pdf" rel="follow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                                upheld
                               </a>
                              </strong>
                              the Department of Agriculture’s decision to allow the organic certification of food grown using hydroponic systems. Nothing in the Organic Foods Production Act of 1990 indicates that hydroponic methods for food production are inconsistent with an organic label.
                             </p>
                            </div>
                           </div>
                          </div>
                         </div>
                        </div>
                       </div>
                       <div class="elementor-column elementor-col-20 elementor-inner-column elementor-element elementor-element-9ca8929" data-element_type="column" data-id="9ca8929" data-settings='{"background_background":"classic"}'>
                        <div class="elementor-column-wrap elementor-element-populated">
                         <div class="elementor-widget-wrap">
                          <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-9ef0c73 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="9ef0c73" data-widget_type="heading.default">
                           <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                            <h1 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">
                             <a data-wpel-link="internal" href="https://www.courthousenews.com/occupy-wall-street-2/" rel="follow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                              Occupy Wall Street
                             </a>
                            </h1>
                           </div>
                          </div>
                          <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-4b36b37 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-element_type="widget" data-id="4b36b37" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
                           <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                            <div class="elementor-text-editor elementor-clearfix">
                             <p>
                              The Second Circuit
                              <strong>
                               <a data-wpel-link="internal" href="https://www.courthousenews.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/occupy-wall-street.pdf" rel="follow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                                ruled
                               </a>
                              </strong>
                              that a trial court improperly instructed a jury on assault claims against a police officer arising from the Occupy Wall Street demonstrations. While New York law allows the use of reasonable force by police for crowd control, the justification charge given to the jury indicated the officer’s subjective intent could be considered, which is contrary to the objective standard of assessment in the law. Because that error was prejudicial, a new trial is warranted.
                             </p>
                            </div>
                           </div>
                          </div>
                         </div>
                        </div>
                       </div>
                       <div class="elementor-column elementor-col-20 elementor-inner-column elementor-element elementor-element-88ce0c9" data-element_type="column" data-id="88ce0c9" data-settings='{"background_background":"classic"}'>
                        <div class="elementor-column-wrap elementor-element-populated">
                         <div class="elementor-widget-wrap">
                          <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-2190c31 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="2190c31" data-widget_type="heading.default">
                           <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                            <h1 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">
                             <a data-wpel-link="internal" href="https://www.courthousenews.com/animal-cruelty-3/" rel="follow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                              Animal Cruelty
                             </a>
                            </h1>
                           </div>
                          </div>
                          <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-9c7c0ab elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-element_type="widget" data-id="9c7c0ab" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
                           <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                            <div class="elementor-text-editor elementor-clearfix">
                             <p>
                              A federal judge
                              <strong>
                               <a data-wpel-link="internal" href="https://www.courthousenews.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/animal-cruelty.pdf" rel="follow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                                vacated
                               </a>
                              </strong>
                              a New York man’s convictions for arson and animal abuse after starting porch fires at an ex-girlfriend’s home and dousing her pet rabbit with gasoline, although it was not injured in the fire. The man had a valid challenge to a prospective juror since she was not clear that she could be impartial in the case due to her love of animals.
                             </p>
                            </div>
                           </div>
                          </div>
                         </div>
                        </div>
                       </div>
                       <div class="elementor-column elementor-col-20 elementor-inner-column elementor-element elementor-element-afe1f96" data-element_type="column" data-id="afe1f96" data-settings='{"background_background":"classic"}'>
                        <div class="elementor-column-wrap elementor-element-populated">
                         <div class="elementor-widget-wrap">
                          <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-297b189 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="297b189" data-widget_type="heading.default">
                           <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                            <h1 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">
                             <a data-wpel-link="internal" href="https://www.courthousenews.com/tribal-rights-2/" rel="follow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                              Tribal Rights
                             </a>
                            </h1>
                           </div>
                          </div>
                          <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-ed4936d elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-element_type="widget" data-id="ed4936d" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
                           <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                            <div class="elementor-text-editor elementor-clearfix">
                             <p>
                              A federal judge
                              <strong>
                               <a data-wpel-link="internal" href="https://www.courthousenews.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/tribal-rights.pdf" rel="follow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                                affirmed
                               </a>
                              </strong>
                              dismissal of a lawsuit in which Oregon ranchers sued to prevent the Klamath Tribes from exercising their superior water rights that interfere with irrigation of the ranchers’ lands. The tribes have preexisting authority to control their water rights under an 1864 treaty with the U.S. government.
                             </p>
                            </div>
                           </div>
                          </div>
                         </div>
                        </div>
                       </div>
                       <div class="elementor-column elementor-col-20 elementor-inner-column elementor-element elementor-element-11ee13f" data-element_type="column" data-id="11ee13f">
                        <div class="elementor-column-wrap elementor-element-populated">
                         <div class="elementor-widget-wrap">
                          <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-6b46aa1 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="widget" data-id="6b46aa1" data-widget_type="heading.default">
                           <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                            <h1 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">
                             <a data-wpel-link="internal" href="https://www.courthousenews.com/texas-power/" rel="follow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                              Texas Power
                             </a>
                            </h1>
                           </div>
                          </div>
                          <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-7016878 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-element_type="widget" data-id="7016878" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
                           <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                            <div class="elementor-text-editor elementor-clearfix">
                             <p>
                              The Texas Supreme Court
                              <strong>
                               <a data-wpel-link="internal" href="https://www.courthousenews.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/tx-power.pdf" rel="follow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
                                declined
                               </a>
                              </strong>
                              to wade into a fraud suit against Texas’ independent energy regulator filed by a power generator that invested $2.2 billion in two new power plants in reliance on the regulator’s projections of a shortfall of electricity. These projections were later revised to indicate an excess of generation capacity. However, the Texas Public Utility Commission has exclusive jurisdiction over these claims.
                             </p>
                            </div>
                           </div>
                          </div>
                         </div>
                        </div>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                    </section>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>
              </section>

               <div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
                <div class="elementor-row">
                 <div class="elementor-column elementor-col-100 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-0dabc2b" data-element_type="column" data-id="0dabc2b">

                   <div class="elementor-widget-wrap">

                    <section class="elementor-section elementor-inner-section elementor-element elementor-element-3921a63 elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-element_type="section" data-id="3921a63">
                     <div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
                      <div class="elementor-row">

                        </a>
                        <figcaption class="widget-image-caption wp-caption-text">
                         “The Shard” dominates the London skyline, as seen on this frigid night in early January 2019. The 72-story skyscraper reaches 1,016 feet into the sky, making it the tallest building in the United Kingdom and the seventh tallest in Europe. It currently houses a hotel, several restaurants, the Warwick Business School, numerous law offices including Greenberg Traurig, and the largest Al Jazeera broadcasting hub outside its home base of Qatar. (Courthouse News photo / William Dotinga)
